They will usually be removed in a later Java release.&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;-XX:PermSize=128m: Ignored in Java 8 and removed in Java 9. PermGen was removed in JDK 8, since Java users should not need to know up front how much memory to reserve for class metadata etc. Just like in the JRockit and J9 JVMs, native memory is now used for class metadata, and it will dynamically grow as needed.
